# FilterTube Tracked File Obligation Index - 2026-05-20

Status: audit-only proof. Runtime behavior is unchanged. This is not an implementation patch.

This index expands `docs/audit/FILTERTUBE_TRACKED_FILE_AUDIT_COVERAGE_2026-05-18.md` from family-level classification into one obligation row for every current `git ls-files` path. It does not prove that each file is complete, optimized, or safe to refactor. It records the minimum future proof each tracked file must cite before behavior, release, website, generated, vendor, or documentation changes rely on that file.

Completion is not proven. Every row remains `obligation-open` until a future feature-specific patch cites positive, negative, route/mode, source-confidence, side-effect, teardown/restore, package, or public-claim proof as applicable.

## Source Universe

```text
git ls-files
156 tracked source files outside docs/audit and tests
```

Ignored raw captures and generated output remain outside this index. If any path below changes family, starts affecting runtime, or becomes generated/release source, this index and its test must change in the same patch.

Static HTML/support script surface addendum: `docs/audit/FILTERTUBE_STATIC_HTML_SUPPORT_SCRIPT_SURFACE_CURRENT_BEHAVIOR_2026-05-21.md` and `tests/runtime/static-html-support-script-surface-current-behavior.test.mjs` add current-behavior proof for the open rows `html/popup.html`, `html/tab-view.html`, `html/troubleshoot.html`, and `scripts/compress-video.swift`. This does not close those rows: popup and dashboard still need loader-order, CSP/resource, route-state, external-navigation, package, and UI smoke proof; `html/troubleshoot.html` still needs a surface decision because it is empty and has no current product opener; and `scripts/compress-video.swift` still needs dry-run, atomic output, and failure-mode proof because it deletes existing output before export success.
